    WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'InProgress'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'Completed'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'Cancelled'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'UnderReview'
    ELSE CAST(`p1`.`Status` AS char)
END AS `Status`, `p1`.`CreateAt`, (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM `Sessions` AS `s`
    WHERE `s`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL AND (`p1`.`Id` = `s`.`CaseId`)) AS `TotalSessions`, (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM `CaseRequests` AS `c1`
    WHERE (`c1`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL AND (`p1`.`Id` = `c1`.`PatientCaseId`)) AND (`c1`.`Status` = 0)) AS `PendingRequests`
FROM (
    SELECT `p`.`Id`, `p`.`CaseTypeId`, `p`.`CreateAt`, `p`.`PatientId`, `p`.`PublicId`, `p`.`Status`
    FROM `PatientCases` AS `p`
    WHERE `p`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
    ORDER BY `p`.`CreateAt` DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS `p1`
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT `p0`.`UserId`, `p0`.`Age`, `p0`.`PublicId`
    FROM `Patients` AS `p0`
    WHERE `p0`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
) AS `p2` ON `p1`.`PatientId` = `p2`.`UserId`
INNER JOIN `AspNetUsers` AS `a` ON `p2`.`UserId` = `a`.`Id`
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT `c`.`Id`, `c`.`Description`, `c`.`Name`, `c`.`PublicId`
    FROM `CaseTypes` AS `c`
    WHERE `c`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
) AS `c0` ON `p1`.`CaseTypeId` = `c0`.`Id`

FROM (
    SELECT `p`.`PublicId`, `p1`.`PublicId` AS `PublicId0`, `a`.`FullName`, `p1`.`Age`, `c0`.`PublicId` AS `PublicId1`, `c0`.`Name`, `c0`.`Description`, CASE `p`.`Status`
        WHEN 0 THEN 'Pending'
        WHEN 1 THEN 'InProgress'
        WHEN 2 THEN 'Completed'
        WHEN 3 THEN 'Cancelled'
        WHEN 4 THEN 'UnderReview'
        ELSE CAST(`p`.`Status` AS char)
    END AS `c`, `p`.`CreateAt`, (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM `Sessions` AS `s`
        WHERE `s`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL AND (`p`.`Id` = `s`.`CaseId`)) AS `c0`, (
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM `CaseRequests` AS `c1`
        WHERE (`c1`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL AND (`p`.`Id` = `c1`.`PatientCaseId`)) AND (`c1`.`Status` = 0)) AS `c1`, `p`.`Id`, `p1`.`UserId`, `a`.`Id` AS `Id0`, `c0`.`Id` AS `Id1`
    FROM `PatientCases` AS `p`
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT `p0`.`UserId`, `p0`.`Age`, `p0`.`PublicId`
        FROM `Patients` AS `p0`
        WHERE `p0`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
    ) AS `p1` ON `p`.`PatientId` = `p1`.`UserId`
    INNER JOIN `AspNetUsers` AS `a` ON `p1`.`UserId` = `a`.`Id`
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT `c`.`Id`, `c`.`Description`, `c`.`Name`, `c`.`PublicId`
        FROM `CaseTypes` AS `c`
        WHERE `c`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
    ) AS `c0` ON `p`.`CaseTypeId` = `c0`.`Id`
    WHERE `p`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL AND (`p`.`PublicId` = @__publicId_0)
    LIMIT 1
) AS `s0`
LEFT JOIN (

    FROM `Medias` AS `m`
    WHERE `m`.`DeleteAt` IS NULL
) AS `m0` ON `s0`.`Id` = `m0`.`PatientCaseId`
